<p><em>Release date: December 10, 2024</em></p>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ”² <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.metric"><code>st.metric</code></a> and <a href="/develop/api-reference/layout/st.columns"><code>st.columns</code></a> have a parameter to show an optional border (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9927">#9927</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9928">#9928</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¨Â Text and background color in <a href="/develop/api-reference/text/st.markdown">Markdown</a> can use the &quot;primary&quot; color from the <code>theme.primaryColor</code> configuration option (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9676">#9676</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¥¶Â You can freeze columns with <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config">column configuration</a> to make them always visible when scrolling horizontally (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9535">#9535</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7078">#7078</a>).</li>
<li>3ï¸âƒ£ The <code>type</code> parameter for <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.button">buttons</a> accepts a new option, <code>&quot;tertiary&quot;</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9923">#9923</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸš¶â€â™‚ï¸Â Streamlit supports <code>pathlib.Path</code> objects everywhere you can use a string path (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9711">#9711</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9783">#9783</a>).</li>
<li>â±ï¸Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.date_input"><code>st.date_input</code></a> and <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.time_input"><code>st.time_input</code></a> accept ISO formatted strings for initial values (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9753">#9753</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’¬Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/write-magic/st.write_stream"><code>st.write_stream</code></a> accepts async generators, which it converts internally to sync generators (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8724">#8724</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8161">#8161</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸªµ The <a href="/develop/api-reference/configuration/config.toml#client"><code>client.showErrorDetails</code></a> configuration option has additional values to show or hide more information (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9909">#9909</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ”Â When Streamlit shows stack traces in the app for uncaught exceptions, internal code is omitted or reduced for easier debugging (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9913">#9913</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ“ˆÂ <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.line_chart"><code>st.line_chart</code></a> shows tooltips for the nearest point on hover (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9674">#9674</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒÂ <a href="/develop/api-reference/utilities/st.html"><code>st.html</code></a> will attempt to convert non-string objects with <code>._repr_html_()</code> before falling back to <code>str()</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9877">#9877</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Streamlit supports Python 3.13 and no longer supports Python 3.8 (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9635">#9635</a>).</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ”£ Material Symbols have been updated with the latest icons (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9813">#9813</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9810">#9810</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ‘½Â Streamlit supports Watchdog version 6 (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9785">#9785</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/RubenVanEldik">RubenVanEldik</a>.</li>
<li>ğŸŒ€Â Bug fix: Streamlit only shows cached function spinners on cache misses and doesn&#x27;t show spinners for nested cached functions (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9956">#9956</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9951">#9951</a>).</li>

<p><em>Release date: November 6, 2024</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ’ŠÂ Introducing <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.pills"><code>st.pills</code></a> to create a single- or multi-select group of pill-buttons.</li>
<li>ğŸ›ï¸Â Introducing <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.segmented_control"><code>st.segmented_control</code></a> to create a segmented button or button group.</li>
<li>ğŸ¤Â Announcing the general availability of <a href="/[...slug]"><code>st.audio_input</code></a>, a widget to let users record sound with their microphones.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>â¡ï¸Â Markdown renders a limited set of typographical symbols (arrows and comparators).</li>
<li><img src="/logo.svg" style="display:inline-block;width:1em"/> You can use <code>:streamlit:</code> to render the Streamlit logo in <a href="/develop/api-reference/text/st.markdown">Markdown</a>.</li>
<li>ğŸÂ <a href="/develop/api-reference/text/st.text"><code>st.text</code></a> wraps text and no longer uses monospace font.</li>
<li>ğŸª£Â You can set <code>use_container_width</code> for <a href="/develop/api-reference/media/st.image"><code>st.image</code></a>. <code>use_column_width</code> is deprecated.</li>
<li>ğŸ“… <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.date_input"><code>st.date_input</code></a> infers the first day of the week from the userâ€™s locale (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9706">#9706</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/5215">#5215</a>).</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ¶Â Streamlitâ€™s CLI tool accepts array values for configuration options (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9577">#9577</a>).</li>
<li>â›“ï¸Â Static file serving supports symlinks (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9147">#9147</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9146">#9146</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/link89">link89</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸš€Â Streamlit provides helpful links for deployment when an app is running locally (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9681">#9681</a>).</li>
<li>â†•ï¸Â The fullscreen button for charts matches with the dataframe toolbar (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9721">#9721</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸƒÂ The running-man icon has a brief delay before rendering to avoid an unnecessary flicker for fast running apps (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9732">#9732</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ–‡ï¸Â The <code>ComponentRequestHandler</code> allows symlinks (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9588">#9588</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ‘†Â Streamlit works with <code>pillow</code> version 11 (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9742">#9742</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/hauntsaninja">hauntsaninja</a>!</li>

<p><em>Release date: October 1, 2024</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ¤Â Introducing <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.audio_input"><code>st.experimental_audio_input</code></a> to let users record with their microphones!</li>
<li>ğŸ“Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.pydeck_chart#chart-selections"><code>st.pydeck_chart</code></a> can return selection events!</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ˜ƒ <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.button"><code>st.button</code></a>, <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.download_button"><code>st.download_button</code></a>, <a href="/develop/api-reference/execution-flow/st.form_submit_button"><code>st.form_submit_button</code></a>, <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.link_button"><code>st.link_button</code></a>, and <a href="/develop/api-reference/layout/st.popover"><code>st.popover</code></a> each have a new parameter to add an icon.</li>
<li>ğŸ¢ <a href="/develop/api-reference/media/st.logo"><code>st.logo</code></a> has a new parameter to adjust the size of your logo.</li>
<li>ğŸ§­ <a href="/develop/api-reference/navigation/st.navigation"><code>st.navigation</code></a> lets you display an always-expanded or collapsible menu using a new <code>expanded</code> parameter.</li>
<li>â†•ï¸Â You can set <code>height</code> and <code>width</code> for <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.map"><code>st.map</code></a> and <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.pydeck_chart"><code>st.pydeck_chart</code></a>.</li>
<li>â†©ï¸Â Form submission behavior can be configured with a new <code>enter_to_submit</code> parameter (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9480">#9480</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7538">#7538</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9406">#9406</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8042">#8042</a>).</li>
<li>â±ï¸ A new config option, <code>server.disconnectedSessionTTL</code>, lets you set a minimum time before a disconnected session is cleaned up (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9179">#9179</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¤¹ Dataframes support multi-index headers (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9483">#9483</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6319">#6319</a>).</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ”‘Â Widget keys appear as HTML classes in the DOM with an <code>st-key-</code> prefix (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9295">#9295</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/5437">#5437</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/3888">#3888</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ”Â The <code>StreamlitAPIException</code> class has been extended into more specific exceptions for some of the most common errors (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9318">#9318</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ—ºï¸ <code>st.map</code> and <code>st.pydeck_chart</code> have a full-screen toggle that matches the dataframe toolbar.</li>

<li>ğŸ•µï¸Â Streamlit is compatible with Watchdog version 5 (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9354">#9354</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/RubenVanEldik">RubenVanEldik</a>!</li>

<p><em>Release date: August 27, 2024</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ“ˆÂ Streamlit natively supports more dataframe formats! Use dataframe and series objects from popular libraries like Dask, Modin, Numpy, pandas, Polars, PyArrow, Snowpark, Xarray, and more. Use database cursors compliant with the Python Database API Specification 2.0. Use anything that supports the Python dataframe interchange protocol. See the <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.dataframe">docs</a>.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>â†”ï¸Â You can control the initial expansion state of <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.json"><code>st.json</code></a> elements.</li>
<li>ğŸ§‘â€ğŸ’»Â You can choose to wrap lines in <a href="/develop/api-reference/text/st.code"><code>st.code</code></a>.</li>
<li>ğŸ•µï¸Â Streamlit supports Kubernetes style secrets so you can use Snowflake Snowpark Container Services secret format (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9078">#9078</a>).</li>
<li>â¤´ï¸Â Breaking change: We removed a patch that allows custom validators in <code>pydantic&lt;2.0</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9257">#9257</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’”Â Breaking change: We removed the experimental cache replay feature from caching decorators (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9305">#9305</a>).</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸŒÂ For better app efficiency, a WebSocket reconnect will not trigger a rerun unless a script run was interrupted (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9083">#9083</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ‘‹Â We updated our <code>streamlit hello</code> app to use Google Material icons.</li>
<li>âŒ¨ï¸Â <code>st.number_input</code>, <code>st.selectbox</code>, <code>st.slider</code>, <code>st.select_slider</code>, and <a href="http://st.radio"><code>st.radio</code></a> provide more precise type hinting for their return values (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9048">#9048</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9296">#9296</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8717">#8717</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/Asaurus1">Asaurus1</a>!</li>
<li>â­Â <a href="http://st.feedback"><code>st.feedback</code></a> provides more precise type hinting for its return value (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9216">#9216</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/wyattscarpenter">wyattscarpenter</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ’…Â We improved theme management for embedded apps viaÂ <code>postMessage</code>Â (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9103">#9103</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒ±Â Bug fix: Within the sidebar, the image for <code>st.logo</code> resizes along with the sidebar width (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9298">#9298</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8707">#8707</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª¹Â Bug fix: When a parent fragment updates, Streamlit cleans up child fragments correctly (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9246">#9246</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9233">#9233</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9267">#9267</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’©Â Bug fix: Elements unstale within a fragment rerun as they are updated instead of all together at the end of the fragment rerun (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9285">#9285</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª±Â Bug fix: If a block type changes during a rerun, Streamlit discards the child elements of that block to prevent improper visual artifacts, like <code>st.tabs</code> causing a blank page (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9276">#9276</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9259">#9259</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8676">#8676</a>).</li>
<li>â˜ ï¸Â Bug fix: Widget state is preserved when page reruns are interrupted with another rerun (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9187">#9187</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9163">#9163</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/dannyopts">dannyopts</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ‘½Â Bug fix: <code>options</code>Â inÂ <code>st.selectbox</code>,Â <code>st.multiselect</code>,Â <code>st.radio</code>, andÂ <code>st.select_slider</code> correctly use <code>dict_items</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9241">#9241</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9237">#9237</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/5377">#5377</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ‘»Â Bug fix: A <code>SelectboxColumn</code> index will show with the correct, grayed-out styling in a dataframe (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9231">#9231</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8772">#8772</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦€Â Bug fix: <code>st.write_stream</code> will not immediately fail when receiving an empty chunk (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9234">#9234</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9227">#9227</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‹Â Bug fix: Streamlit won&#x27;t auto-scroll to an empty anchor, if present (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9206">#9206</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9203">#9203</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦Â Bug fix: We changed the handling of <code>scriptRunId</code> to prevent <code>st.tabs</code> from showing extra, empty tabs in fragments (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9186">#9186</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9158">#9158</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9215">#9215</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒÂ Bug fix: Automatically rerunning fragments don&#x27;t raise <code>FragmentStorageKeyError</code> to prevent a possible race condition (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9183">#9183</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9080">#9080</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•¸ï¸Â Bug fix: We improved <code>st.plotly_chart</code>&#x27;s handling of the pass-through keyword argument <code>config</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9190">#9190</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9134">#9134</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦—Â Bug fix: Markdown in all <code>label</code> parameters correctly ignores headers (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9189">#9189</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9141">#9141</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‚Â Bug fix: We reverted a change to fragments which caused some widgets to lose state in some circumstances (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9178">#9178</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9171">#9171</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ŸÂ Bug fix: The deprecation warnings for <code>st.experimental_fragment</code> and <code>st.experimental_dialog</code> only show when the commands are called. This prevents custom components which use them from raising premature warnings on import (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9170">#9170</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/9143">#9143</a>).</li>

<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: You can now clear the cache for cached class instance methods (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/9101">#9101</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8638">#8638</a>).</li>

<p><em>Release date: July 25, 2024</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸª Introducing <a href="/develop/api-reference/utilities/st.context"><code>st.context</code></a> to read headers and cookies!</li>
<li>â­ Introducing <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.feedback"><code>st.feedback</code></a> to collect ratings and sentiment from your users!</li>
<li>ğŸ‘ŸÂ Announcing the general availability of <a href="/develop/api-reference/execution-flow/st.fragment"><code>st.fragment</code></a>, a decorator that lets you rerun functions independently of the whole page.</li>
<li>ğŸ¿Â Announcing the general availability of <a href="/develop/api-reference/execution-flow/st.dialog"><code>st.dialog</code></a>, a decorator that lets you create modal dialogs.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>â„¹ï¸ You can use icons from the Material Symbols library in <a href="/develop/api-reference/text/st.markdown">Markdown</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ“ˆÂ You can pass <code>graphviz.Source</code> objects to <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.graphviz_chart"><code>st.graphviz_chart</code></a>.</li>
<li>ğŸ“Š You can modify the stacking behavior for <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.bar_chart"><code>st.bar_chart</code></a> and <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.area_chart"><code>st.area_chart</code></a>.</li>
<li>ğŸ”­Â Within a fragment, you can scope <a href="/develop/api-reference/execution-flow/st.rerun"><code>st.rerun</code></a> to the fragment.</li>
<li>ğŸªºÂ Streamlit supports nested fragments (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8931">#8931</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8635">#8635</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ“Â Fragments can be used in callback functions (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8916">#8916</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8591">#8591</a>).</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>â­• Material Symbols are rounded instead of outlined (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8998">#8998</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ”¢Â Streamlit supports Numpy version 2.0 (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8940">#8940</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ˜„Â We&#x27;ve updated emoji validation for new emojis (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8923">#8923</a>).</li>

<p><em>Release date: June 20, 2024</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ§­ Introducing <a href="/develop/api-reference/navigation/st.navigation"><code>st.navigation</code></a> and <a href="/develop/api-reference/navigation/st.page"><code>st.Page</code></a> for a new way to define multipage apps! Check out the <a href="/develop/concepts/multipage-apps/overview">docs</a> to learn more.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ“ŠÂ <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.bar_chart"><code>st.bar_chart</code></a> can render charts horizontally.</li>
<li>â„¹ï¸Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/layout/st.expander"><code>st.expander</code></a> supports adding an icon next to its label.</li>
<li>ğŸ—ï¸Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/layout/st.columns"><code>st.columns</code></a> lets you set vertical alignment.</li>
<li>ğŸ“² Custom components support callback functions (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8633">#8633</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/3977">#3977</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ“¥ Fragments no longer support rendering widgets outside of their main body (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8756">#8756</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ·ï¸ You can now customize axis labels for <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.area_chart"><code>st.area_chart</code></a>, <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.bar_chart"><code>st.bar_chart</code></a>, <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.line_chart"><code>st.line_chart</code></a>, and <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.scatter_chart"><code>st.scatter_chart</code></a>.</li>
<li>âŒ› The caching parameter <code>experimental_allow_widgets</code> is deprecated (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8817">#8817</a>).</li>
<li>âŒ Streamlit no longer supports legacy caching. <code>st.cache</code> is now an alias for <code>st.cache_data</code> and <code>st.cache_resource</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8737">#8737</a>).</li>
<li>â¬†ï¸ Streamlit supports <code>protobuf</code> version 5 (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8627">#8627</a>).</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>âœ¨Â Streamlit Hello uses <code>st.navigation</code> and <code>st.Page</code>, the new, preferred method for declaring multipage apps (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8806">#8806</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ§¹Â Streamlit no longer appends &quot;Â· Streamlit&quot; to the page title of apps, unless running on Community Cloud (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8900">#8900</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‹Â Streamlit magic and <code>st.write</code> use <code>st.json</code> to display <code>st.secrets</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8659">#8659</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/2905">#2905</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ”Â Streamlit doesn&#x27;t automatically check for newer version on PyPi (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8841">#8841</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8453">#8453</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒÂ Bug fix: Custom component functions require importing <code>streamlit.components.v1</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8666">#8666</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8644">#8644</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•¸ï¸Â Bug fix: Reverted change to handle Altairs <code>resolve_scale</code> method since it caused a regression (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8845">#8845</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8642">#8642</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦—Â Bug fix: Images in Markdown do not overflow the Markdown container (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8794">#8794</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‚Â Bug fix: Clarified the error message for <code>st.selectbox</code> when <code>index</code> is larger than the size of <code>options</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8775">#8775</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8771">#8771</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ŸÂ Bug fix: Streamlit correctly handles non-widget elements with IDs (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8770">#8770</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8768">#8768</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ Â Bug fix: Docstrings correctly identify when <code>use_container_width=True</code> is the default (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8809">#8809</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª°Â Bug fix: Streamlit has a consistent minimum element height for better vertical alignment (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8797">#8797</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8835">#8835</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8027">#8027</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8706">#8706</a>).</li>

<p><em>Release date: May 23, 2024</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ“ˆÂ Announcing user selections for charts! Use <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.plotly_chart"><code>st.plotly_chart</code></a>, <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.altair_chart"><code>st.altair_chart</code></a>, and <a href="/develop/api-reference/charts/st.vega_lite_chart"><code>st.vega_lite_chart</code></a> to make chart widgets for even more interactive apps.</li>
<li>ğŸš£â€â™‚ï¸ Announcing user selections for dataframes. Get row and column selections from users with <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.dataframe"><code>st.dataframe</code></a>.</li>
<li>ğŸ’¼Â Introducing <a href="/develop/api-reference/media/st.logo"><code>st.logo</code></a> to add an image in the sidebar, above navigation.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ”—Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.page_link"><code>st.page_link</code></a> supports Material icons (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8593">#8593</a>).</li>
<li>âš“Â Anchor button for headers display inline at the end of headers for a more beautiful and consistent appearance (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8587">#8587</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸˆ‚ï¸Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/connections/st.connections.sqlconnection"><code>SQLConnection</code></a> accepts <code>query</code> as a <code>sqlalchemy.URL.create</code> parameter so you can specify character sets (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8581">#8581</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/LucianLiu6">LucianLiu6</a>!</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ•¸ï¸Â Bug fix: A fallback method was added for CSV downloads to increase browser compatibility (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8452">#8452</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8210">#8210</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦—Â Bug fix: Column config is deep-copied when cloned to prevent unintentional modifications (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8677">#8677</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‚Â Bug fix: <code>st.data_editor</code> renders correctly when using <code>num_rows=dynamic</code> with null values in added rows (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8640">#8640</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7458">#7458</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ŸÂ Bug fix: <code>streamlit run</code> will display the <code>localhost</code> address when initializing Streamlit with <code>server.headless=true</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8647">#8647</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8629">#8629</a>).</li>

<p><em>Release date: May 2, 2024</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ¿Â Introducing <code>st.experimental_dialog</code>! Create a modal overlay that can also rerun independently from the rest of your app. Check out the <a href="/develop/api-reference/execution-flow/st.dialog">docs</a> to learn how.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ”£Â <code>st.toast</code>, <code>st.chat_message</code>, <code>st.set_page_config</code>, <code>st.info</code>, <code>st.success</code>, <code>st.error</code>, and <code>st.warning</code> can use Google Material Symbols for their icons.</li>
<li>ğŸŒˆÂ <a href="/develop/api-reference/text/st.markdown">Markdown</a> supports background colors for text. Check out the <a href="https://background-colors.streamlit.app/">feature demo app</a>.</li>
<li>ğŸ¥Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/media/st.audio"><code>st.audio</code></a> and <a href="/develop/api-reference/media/st.video"><code>st.video</code></a> can now be set to autoplay. <code>st.video</code> can be muted.</li>
<li>ğŸ—ƒï¸Â You can <a href="/develop/api-reference/caching-and-state/st.cache_data#cachedfuncclear">clear specific cached values</a> for a cached function. Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/OscarSaharoy">OscarSaharoy</a>!</li>
<li>â“Â You can now set all query parameters with a single call to <a href="/develop/api-reference/caching-and-state/st.query_params#stquery_paramsfrom_dict"><code>st.query_params.from_dict</code></a>. Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/Asaurus1">Asaurus1</a>!</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ”²Â Streamlit supports Modin and Snowpark pandas DataFrames and Series (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8506">#8506</a>).</li>
<li>â±ï¸Â Improved support for <code>period</code> data types in <code>st.dataframe</code> and <code>st.data_editor</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7987">#7987</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ—ºï¸Â Streamlit supports using <code>pydeck-carto</code> with <code>st.pydeck_chart</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8422">#8422</a>).</li>
<li>â„ï¸Â Additional <code>snowflake</code> requirements were updated to allow Python versions 3.8 to 3.11 (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8538">#8538</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ <code>st.toast</code> received visual improvements and now appears in the top right (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8433">#8433</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‹Â Visual tweaks for dialogs and modals.</li>
<li>ğŸ¦€Â Bug fix: <code>st.write_stream</code> returns an empty string when passed a generator with no yield (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8560">#8560</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦Â Bug fix: Widgets that support <code>None</code> values can be correctly set to <code>None</code> through Session State (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8529">#8529</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7649">#7649</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒÂ Bug fix: If the initial value for <code>st.date_input</code> is not set and today&#x27;s date falls outside the declared minimum or maximum, then the minimum or maximum will be used instead, whichever is closer (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8519">#8519</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6167">#6167</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•¸ï¸Â Bug fix: Altair&#x27;s <code>resolve_scale</code> method is handled correctly (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8497">#8497</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/1667">#1667</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦—Â Bug fix: <code>st.multiselects</code> correctly handles sets when passed to <code>options</code> or <code>default</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8471">#8471</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8466">#8466</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‚Â Bug fix: <code>st.status</code> does not show the expander toggle when empty (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8369">#8369</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ŸÂ Bug fix: The width of <code>vconcat</code> charts in Vega and Altair is set correctly (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8498">#8498</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/2751">#2751</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ Â Bug fix: Apps print beautifully and no longer show excessive whitespace (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8502">#8502</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7815">#7815</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª°Â Bug fix: Invalid escape sequences were removed to avoid warnings from <code>pytest</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8510">#8510</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8501">#8501</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª³Â Bug fix: <code>st.file_uploader</code> callback is correctly executed once per file selection after the first selection (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8493">#8493</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/4877">#4877</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•·ï¸Â Bug fix: Streamlit is compatible down to <code>pillow</code> version 7.1.0 instead of 9.1.0 (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8492">#8492</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8486">#8486</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: Widget values are correctly dropped when a script run is interrupted by switching pages (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8425">#8425</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7338">#7338</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: Apps in dark mode will return to dark mode after printing (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8469">#8469</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7879">#7879</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸœÂ Bug fix: Component ready state is dynamic to avoid race conditions that caused blank apps in Safari (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8434">#8434</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8362">#8362</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª²Â Bug fix: <code>st.slider</code> yields a Python error when <code>min_value</code> is less than or equal to <code>max_value</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8413">#8413</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8342">#8342</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ›Â Bug fix: Time is offset correctly for Vega and Altair (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8278">#8278</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/4342">#4342</a>).</li>
</ul>

<p><em>Release date: April 4, 2024</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ‘ŸÂ Introducing <a href="/develop/api-reference/execution-flow/st.fragment"><code>st.experimental_fragment</code></a> to decorate functions and rerun them independently of the whole page. Check out the <a href="/develop/concepts/architecture/fragments">docs</a> and give your apps a speed boost!</li>
<li>ğŸŒÂ Introducing <code>st.html</code> to insert custom HTML into your app! Check out the <a href="/develop/api-reference/utilities/st.html">docs</a> for how to use it.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ“ºÂ <a href="/develop/api-reference/media/st.audio"><code>st.audio</code></a> and <a href="/develop/api-reference/media/st.video"><code>st.video</code></a> allow looping and setting an end time (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8203">#8203</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8348">#8348</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ”Â <code>AppTest</code> allows switching pages with <a href="/develop/api-reference/app-testing/st.testing.v1.apptest#apptestswitch_page"><code>AppTest.switch_page</code></a> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8280">#8280</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ§ª <code>format_func</code> is accessible in <code>AppTest</code> for widgets that use it (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8189">#8189</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8019">#8019</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7679">#7679</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ“ˆ Column configuration now includes <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config/st.column_config.areachartcolumn"><code>AreaChartColumn</code></a>. <a href="/develop/api-reference/data/st.column_config/st.column_config.linechartcolumn"><code>LineChartColumn</code></a> no longer shows area (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8237">#8237</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸš§ Breaking change: <a href="/develop/api-reference/write-magic/st.write"><code>st.write</code></a> will no longer set <code>unsafe_allow_html=True</code> when passed an object containing a <code>_repr_html_</code> method. For more information, see PR <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8238">#8238</a>.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ–±ï¸Users can click on the widget label to focus on input for <code>st.number_input</code>, <code>st.text_input</code>, and <code>st.text_area</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8155">#8155</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/filiptammergard">filiptammergard</a>!</li>
<li>â¬†ï¸ Streamlit supports <code>packaging</code> version 24.x (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8338">#8338</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8328">#8328</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•¸ï¸Â Bug fix: Streamlit now watches for changes to imported modules in addition to pages (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8372">#8372</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/zyxue">zyxue</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ¦—Â Bug fix: Overflowing toast messages are correctly truncated (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8337">#8337</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8330">#8330</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‚Â Bug fix: <code>st.status</code> correctly updates to complete when using LangChain&#x27;s <code>StreamlitCallbackHandler</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8311">#8331</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦Ÿ Bug fix: Custom components no longer show white backgrounds in dark themes (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8242">#8242</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8156">#8156</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7813">#7813</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦  Bug fix: Content area width is reduced when a fullscreen icon would otherwise cause horizontal overflow (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8279">#8279</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6990">#6990</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª° Bug fix: Custom components with undefined frame heights will render with a height of 0 (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8290">#8290</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8285">#8285</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª³Â Bug fix: Restored a check for active sessions to prevent apps from needlessly running when no users are connected (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8294">#8294</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•·ï¸ Bug fix: Custom themes have precedence over embedding options (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8021">#8021</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7118">#7118</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: Reverted the async timer to expire session storage cache to address computational efficiency (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8281">#8281</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: When using <code>st.popover</code> with <code>use_container_width=True</code>, the popover container&#x27;s minimum width will match the popover button (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8266">#8266</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8261">#8261</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸœ Bug fix: Using <code>st.rerun</code> with a triggering widget in <code>AppTest</code> no longer creates an infinite loop (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8264">#8264</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7768">#7768</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª²Â Bug fix: URLs are correctly decoded in <code>LinkColumn</code> if regex is used or if not using fully qualified URLs (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8258">#8258</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7064">#7064</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ›Â Bug fix: <code>st.query_params</code> only sends one <code>ForwardMsg</code> when updating multiple parameters (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8205">#8205</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8199">#8199</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/Asaurus1">Asaurus1</a>!</li>
</ul>

<p><em>Release date: March 7, 2024</em></p>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ¿Â Introducing <code>st.popover</code> to create popover elements in your Streamlit apps. Check out <a href="/develop/api-reference/layout/st.popover">the docs</a> to see how to use it!</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ“ºÂ You can now pass subtitles to <a href="/develop/api-reference/media/st.video"><code>st.video</code></a>! Check out our <a href="https://doc-video-subtitle-inputs.streamlit.app/">feature demo</a>.</li>
<li>âš—ï¸Â <a href="/develop/api-reference/app-testing/st.testing.v1.apptest"><code>AppTest</code></a> includes support for <code>st.expander</code> and <code>st.status</code>.</li>
<li>ğŸ§ªÂ <a href="/develop/api-reference/app-testing/st.testing.v1.apptest#apptestfrom_function"><code>AppTest.from_function</code></a> accepts a function that takes arguments and/or returns a value.</li>
<li>ğŸ§©Â The timeout warning for custom components was replaced with an element skeleton to improve the UX for slow-loading components, especially in some cloud-hosted platforms (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8179">#8179</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7046">#7046</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ“„ <code>st.switch_page</code> and <code>st.page_link</code> received significant improvements to path handling, performance, and visual appearance (see below for details).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦€Â Bug fix: Streamlit uses <code>glide-data-grid</code> version 6.0.4 to fix a variety of dataframe issues (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7779">#7779</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6900">#6900</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7032">#7032</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7727">#7727</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6810">#6810</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7930">#7930</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7949">#7949</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7831">#7831</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8168">#8168</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’¦ Bug fix: We&#x27;ve plugged a significant memory leak in the coroutine loop. Apps that generate a large number of small messages between client and server will benefit greatly (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8068">#8068</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7989">#7989</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6510">#6510</a>).</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ’ª Multiple modules are now lazy-loaded to speed up Streamlit&#x27;s import time (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8150">#8150</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8143">#8143</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8134">#8134</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8113">#8113</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8125">#8125</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8111">#8111</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8109">#8109</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6066">#6066</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ–¼ï¸Â <code>st.write</code> supports <code>PIL</code> images (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8039">#8039</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ”—Â <code>st.radio</code> allows markdown links within the items passed to <code>options</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8028">#8028</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7992">#7992</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’€Â TheÂ <code>deprecation.showPyplotGlobalUse</code> config option is deprecated and will be removed in the subsequent release (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8133">#8133</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¤–Â Streamlit supports AzureOpenAI chat stream (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8107">#8107</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8084">#8084</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒÂ The <code>/healthz</code> endpoint supports the HTTP HEAD method (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8145">#8145</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8144">#8144</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/rahulmistri1997">rahulmistri1997</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸŒ€Â The <code>cache</code> parameter forÂ <code>st.spinner</code> is now private (<code>_cache</code>) since it&#x27;s for internal use (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8118">#8118</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸƒÂ Session storage is checked and expired asynchronously to improve performance and efficiency of apps with lower traffic (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8083">#8083</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸœÂ <code>st.write_stream</code> raises a descriptive <code>Exception</code> when the message cannot be parsed (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8036">#8036</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ“˜Â Fixed a typo in the examples for <code>st.switch_page</code> and <code>st.page_link</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8162">#8162</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/t1emp0">t1emp0</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ‘»Â Bug fix:Â <code>st.help</code> correctly displays conditional members (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8228">#8228</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‹Â Bug fix: App State fully clears on page change to prevent lingering stale elements (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8208">#8208</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦Â Bug fix: <code>st.info</code>, <code>st.success</code>, <code>st.warning</code>, and <code>st.error</code> don&#x27;t overflow with long markdown strings (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8194">#8194</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6394">#6394</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒÂ Bug fix: Streamlit shows a warning that port 3000 is reserved for development when the server port is set to 3000 (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8152">#8152</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8149">#8149</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•¸ï¸Â Bug fix: <code>st.page_link</code> and <code>st.switch_page</code> have improved path calculation for consistency (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8127">#8127</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦—Â Bug fix: <code>st.page_link</code> shows the correct path in browser on hover (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8086">#8086</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8080">#8080</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦‚Â Bug fix: <code>st.page_link</code> and <code>st.switch_page</code> normalize paths for correct handling in Windows (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8103">#8103</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8070">#8070</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦ŸÂ Bug fix: Script runner uses a while loop instead of recursion to avoid stack overflows (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8100">#8100</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ¦  Bug fix: <code>st.page_link</code> and <code>st.switch_page</code> correctly handle relative paths prefixed with <code>&quot;/&quot;</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8085">#8085</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8081">#8081</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª°Â Bug fix: <code>st.image</code> parses paths in Windows correctly (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8092">#8092</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7271">#7271</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6066">#6066</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª³Â Bug fix: <code>st.switch_page</code> no longer waits for the current page to finish running before switching pages (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8054">#8054</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7954">#7954</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•·ï¸Â Bug fix: <code>st.map</code> and other simple charts correctly handle color when data is not indexed starting from 0 (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8158">#8158</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8079">#8079</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/8077">#8077</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/awhazell">awhazell</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: <code>st.selectbox</code>, <code>st.multiselect</code>, <code>st.select_slider</code>, and <code>st.radio</code> use shallow copies of their options to prevent unexpected mutations (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8064">#8064</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7534">#7534</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: The selected time in <code>st.time_input</code> displays correctly in dark mode (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8056">#8056</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7436">#7436</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª²Â Bug fix: Dataframe scrollbars display correctly in the latest version of Chrome (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8034">#8034</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ›Â Bug fix: Casting <code>st.query_params</code> to <code>str</code> will print the content of the query parameters instead of the class description (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8030">#8030</a>).</li>
</ul>

<p><em>Release date: February 1, 2024</em></p>
<p><strong>Release videos</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=0TSXM-BGqHU">What&#x27;s new?</a></li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ”—Â Introducing <code>st.page_link</code>! Now, you can build custom navigation menus for your multipage apps. Check out <a href="/develop/api-reference/widgets/st.page_link">our docs</a> to see how.</li>
<li>ğŸ’¦Â Announcing <code>st.write_stream</code> to conveniently handle generators and streamed responses. Check out <a href="/develop/api-reference/write-magic/st.write_stream">our docs</a> to see how making chat apps just got easier.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ“Â <code>st.chat_input</code> can be used inline and placed anywhere in the app. You can also have multiple <code>st.chat_input</code> widgets on a page (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7896">#7896</a>).</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ§¹Â Internal refactoring and cleanup (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7980">#7980</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/whitphx">whitphx</a>!</li>
<li>â„ï¸Â Bug fix: Snowpark is now an optional dependency for <code>SnowflakeConnection</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7919">#7919</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•·ï¸Â Bug fix: The watchdog suggestion is disabled when <code>server.fileWatcherType</code> is set to <code>none</code> or <code>poll</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/8024">#8024</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7999">#7999</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: Required columns can be hidden when not using <code>st.data_editor</code> with dynamic rows (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7996">#7996</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7991">#7991</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: New period types are supported for pandas 2.2.0 (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7988">#7988</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸœÂ Bug fix: Custom components receive only the app&#x27;s origin and path to avoid reloading components when query parameters change (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7951">#7951</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7503">#7503</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/eric-skydio">eric-skydio</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸª²Â Bug fix: <code>st.progress</code> won&#x27;t raise an exception when given a value above 1.0 due to float precision (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7953">#7953</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/5517">#5517</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/notiona">notiona</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ“š Streamlit supports<code>importlib-metadata</code> version 7 (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7925">#7925</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/elgalu">elgalu</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸ›Â Bug fix: <code>AppTest</code> correctly sees widgets inside containers (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7923">#7923</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7711">#7711</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’¿ Custom components no longer accumulate style elements when re-rendered for better performance (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7914">#7914</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/Tom-Julux">Tom-Julux</a>!</li>
</ul>

<p><em>Release date: January 11, 2024</em></p>
<p><strong>Release videos</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OIQskkX_DK0">What&#x27;s new?</a></li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Highlights</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ”„Â Announcing <code>st.switch_page</code> to programmatically switch pages in multipage apps! Check out our <a href="/develop/api-reference/navigation/st.switch_page">docs</a> to learn about this highly anticipated feature!</li>
<li>â“Introducing <code>st.query_params</code> to handle variables passed through your app&#x27;s URL. Check out our <a href="/develop/api-reference/caching-and-state/st.query_params">docs</a> to understand this feature and how it&#x27;s been upgraded and improved from our experimental version!</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Notable Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ“Â <code>st.container</code> can be configured with a height to create grids or scrolling containers (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7697">#7697</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/2169">#2169</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/2447">#2447</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ”—Â For dataframes,Â <code>LinkColumn</code>Â has a simplified UI and can be configured with display text, including programmatically defined text through regular expressions (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7784">#7784</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7741">#7741</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6787">#6787</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ§­Â Sidebar navigation for multipage apps can be hidden via configuration (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7852">#7852</a>).</li>
<li>â©Â Plotly figures can load even faster when used in combination with <code>orjson</code> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7860">#7860</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/eric-skydio">eric-skydio</a>!</li>
<li>â™»ï¸ Behavior change: Query parameters are removed when changing pages (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7817">#7817</a>,Â <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/6725">#6725</a>,Â <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/5505">#5505</a>).</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>Other Changes</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>ğŸ› ï¸Â <code>showFooter</code> is no longer an embed option since the footer no longer exists (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7902">#7902</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7785">#7785</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•µï¸ All security concerns should be reported through <a href="https://hackerone.com/snowflake?type=team">HackerOne</a> (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7783">#7783</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ•·ï¸Â Bug fix: Tabs are not disabled when stale to prevent flickering (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7905">#7905</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7820">#7820</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ›¡ï¸Â Bug fix: The full file path is used instead of a prefix to prevent custom components from reaching beyond their own folders (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7901">#7901</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª±Â Bug fix: Widgets raise an exception if its values aren&#x27;t Python comparable (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7840">#7840</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/3714">#3714</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: The down-arrow icons on expanders maintain a consistent size (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7596">#7596</a>). Thanks, <a href="https://github.com/matiboux">matiboux</a>!</li>
<li>ğŸÂ Bug fix: Tabs no longer flicker when switching between them (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7904">#7904</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸœÂ Bug fix: Enter-to-submit is automatically disabled when the associated <code>st.form_submit_button</code> is disabled (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7827">#7827</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7822">#7822</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª²Â Bug fix: Required columns cannot be hidden with column configuration (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7888">#7888</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7559">#7559</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ›Â Bug fix: Using <code>nan</code> as a value in <code>SelectboxColumn</code> will raise an error instead of silently failing (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7887">#7887</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7558">#7558</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸŒ™Â Bug fix: Custom component iframes allow dark mode (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7821">#7821</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7813">#7813</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª°Â Bug fix: The command to start Streamlit is not sent to the frontend (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7787">#7787</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸ’…Â Bug fix: The background color of <code>st.toggle</code> is enhanced for better visibility (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7788">#7788</a>).</li>
<li>ğŸª³Â Bug fix: Built-in charts can handle ordered categorical columns (<a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/pull/7771">#7771</a>, <a href="https://github.com/streamlit/streamlit/issues/7776">#7776</a>).</li>
